                <div class="date-outer">
                 <h2 class="date-header">
                  <span>
                   Wednesday
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div class="date-posts">
                  <div class="post-outer">
                   <div class="post hentry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                    <meta content="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rsyf41YS6hY/VRQmCiza2BI/AAAAAAAAnrM/7W2RwJ_EZXA/s1600/purses20.jpg" itemprop="image_url"/>
                    <meta content="4277755039706557399" itemprop="blogId"/>
                    <meta content="5314386702291526514" itemprop="postId"/>
                    <a name="5314386702291526514">
                    </a>
                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.freedazoshopping.com/2015/04/23-designer-handbags-for-all-ladies.html">
                      23 Designer Handbags For All Ladies
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5314386702291526514" itemprop="articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rsyf41YS6hY/VRQmCiza2BI/AAAAAAAAnrM/7W2RwJ_EZXA/s1600/purses20.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" height="160" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Rsyf41YS6hY/VRQmCiza2BI/AAAAAAAAnrM/7W2RwJ_EZXA/s1600/purses20.jpg" width="320"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Designer Handbags or very expensive purses, are there for you to buy and feel good about yourself. But do you really need them to feel sexy, smart, wanted and rich? Not at all, but you have been so conditioned as a woman by the designers, that you are now compelled to buy into their designs so you could keep making them richer. And because they forced you to believe that you must have the latest purse or designer handbag in order to be part of the in-crowd, the talked - about, and for you to be the envy of other women, that you have to get your hands on the latest purse that carries a heavy price tag. And since I can't stop you, nor help you to change your mind from being a Slave to the exterior influences that are telling you when and how to feel sexy, beautiful and wanted, then this is why today I am sharing with You these 23 Designer Handbags For All Ladies. So Enjoy Your Poison Ladies! But first, did you know that:?
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Sigmund Freud considered handbags and purses to a vaginal symbol.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Yes, even the handbag got sexed-up by Freud, who in
                        </span>
                        <em style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Dora: An Analysis of a Case of Hysteria
                        </em>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         , concluded that his patient's playing with her handbag during therapy actually meant that the bag was a symbol female of genitalia, and all Dora really wanted to do was masturbate.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                        <b>
                         <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2DY3QSnsbUk/VRQqmw0IHcI/AAAAAAAAnt0/Fp-PtL34pYE/s1600/purses25.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                          <img border="0" height="292" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-2DY3QSnsbUk/VRQqmw0IHcI/AAAAAAAAnt0/Fp-PtL34pYE/s1600/purses25.jpg" width="400"/>
                         </a>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         The term 'handbag' didn't exist until the development of the railroad revolutionised luggage.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Women became more mobile, sparking leather artisans to start to creating easier to carry hand-held bags.
                        </span>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="color: red;">
                         <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                          The first luxury leather handbags, as we know them today, were created in 1841 by London's H. J. Cave
                         </span>
                         <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                          . After a request by industrialist and confectionary kingpin Samuel Parkinson, Cave created travel bags for the entire Parkinson family, designing a sturdy yet small bag for Samuel's wife cut from tough leather
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         . They're now on display in the handbag museum in Amsterdam.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                       <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                        <b>
                         <br/>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Miuccia Prada introduced the first totally unisex bag
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         . Designed in 1985, the black nylon knapsack is still somewhat ubiquitous today.
                        </span>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         The most expensive bag to be entered into the Guinness Book of World Records
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         is House of Mouawad's
                         <span style="font-size: large;">
                          '
                         </span>
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         <span style="font-size: large;">
                          1001 Nights Diamond Purse', priced at $34.5 million.
                         </span>
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                        <b>
                         <span style="font-size: large;">
                          <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xSOSOqjSjQ4/VRQq4PCXarI/AAAAAAAAnt8/x-5dtLcJzRg/s1600/purses27.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                           <img border="0" height="210" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-xSOSOqjSjQ4/VRQq4PCXarI/AAAAAAAAnt8/x-5dtLcJzRg/s1600/purses27.jpg" width="640"/>
                          </a>
                         </span>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Handbags came long before pockets.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Coin purses that you could attached to your girdle were invented long before anyone thought to put pockets on trousers and skirts.
                        </span>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Traditionally, bags were entirely a 'man thing'.
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Ancient Egyptian hieroglyphs depict males carrying purse shaped pouches around their waist, while ancient African priests were thought to carry beaded bags. Hello embellishment.
                        </span>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <br style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;"/>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         Clutch bags were originally called 'pochettes'
                        </span>
                        <span style="background-color: white; color: #515151; line-height: 18px; orphans: 2; widows: 2;">
                         , and didn't appear until the early 1900s.
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </span>

                    <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                     <a href="http://www.freedazoshopping.com/2015/03/23-creative-ways-to-use-your-closet.html">
                      23 Creative Ways To Use Your Closet Space
                     </a>
                    </h3>
                    <div class="post-header">
                     <div class="post-header-line-1">
                     </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8919700812922050936" itemprop="articleBody">
                     <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-quqNjxy62vI/VQCG8mJtMOI/AAAAAAAAnBc/M6gOdH8sbcU/s1600/closet2.gif" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                        <img border="0" height="177" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-quqNjxy62vI/VQCG8mJtMOI/AAAAAAAAnBc/M6gOdH8sbcU/s1600/closet2.gif" width="320"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        Your Closet is not only meant for your clothes and shoes to be stored, but it is also a vital part of your house that you can use for just about anything, if you can de-condition your mind from what Society has misled you to believe.
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                       <b>
                        <br/>
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <div class="buzz_superlist_item buzz_superlist_item_image buzz_superlist_item_wide image_hit " id="superlist_3507281_4224194" rel:buzz_num="1" style="background: rgb(255, 255, 255); border: 0px; clear: both; color: #111111; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; font-size: 12px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 20px 0px; position: relative;">
                       <h2 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-size: 26px; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                         <span class="buzz_superlist_number_inline" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; display: inline; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          1.
                         </span>
                         Make a homework space.
                        </span>
                       </h2>

                       <div class="sub_buzz_desc_w_attr" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #222222; font-size: 17px; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 23px; outline: 0px; padding: 14px 0px 12px;">
                        <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                         <b>
                          Build a simple bench, add a cushion, and arrange your childs favorite books to create the perfect reading nook. Get the full tutorial
                          <a href="http://thriftydecorchick.blogspot.com/2011/05/closet-turned-book-nook.html" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #0077ee; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;">
                           here
                          </a>
                          .
                         </b>
                        </span>

                       <h2 style="background: transparent; border: 0px; color: #121212; font-size: 26px; font-stretch: normal; line-height: 28px; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 8px;">
                        <span style="font-family: Georgia, Times New Roman, serif;">
                         <span class="buzz_superlist_number_inline" style="background: transparent; border: 0px; display: inline; margin: 0px; outline: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                          23.
                         </span>
                         Make a family fort.
                        </span>
                       </h2>
